"""KDA forward (chunk form) — optimized PyTorch with batch matmuls.

Uses efficient batch matrix multiplications for the intra-chunk A matrix
(A = k_exp @ k_neg.T with cumulative correction) and the inter-chunk
recurrence.  All compute runs in fp32 for accuracy with bf16 I/O.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
from einops import rearrange


def _kda_forward_pytorch(
    q: torch.Tensor,
    k: torch.Tensor,
    v: torch.Tensor,
    g: torch.Tensor,
    beta: torch.Tensor,
    scale: float,
    chunk_size: int = 64,
) -> torch.Tensor:
    """KDA forward — batch-matmul formulation (fp32 compute, bf16 output)."""
    dtype = v.dtype
    B, T, H, K_dim = q.shape
    V_dim = v.shape[-1]
    BT = chunk_size
    NT = T // BT

    q, k, v, g, beta = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q, k, v, g, beta))
    q = q * scale

    q = rearrange(q, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
    k = rearrange(k, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
    v = rearrange(v, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
    g = rearrange(g, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
    beta = rearrange(beta, "b (n c) h -> b h n c", c=BT)

    g = g.cumsum(-2)

    # ---- Intra-chunk: build A = k_exp @ k_neg.T  (batch matmul) ----
    k_exp = k * g.exp()
    k_neg = k * (-g).exp()
    q_exp = q * g.exp()

    A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
    A = A * beta.unsqueeze(-1)
    A = -A.masked_fill(
        torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=A.device), diagonal=0),
        0.0,
    )

    # Cumulative correction  (I - A)^{-1} - I  via forward substitution
    for i in range(1, BT):
        A_row = A[..., i, :, None]
        A_left = A[..., :, :i]
        A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i] + (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)

    A = (A + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)) * beta.unsqueeze(-2)

    w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
    u = torch.matmul(A, v)

    # ---- Inter-chunk recurrence ----
    S = torch.zeros(B, H, K_dim, V_dim, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)
    o = torch.zeros_like(v)
    mask_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=A.device), diagonal=1)

    for i in range(NT):
        q_i = q[:, :, i]
        k_i = k[:, :, i]
        u_i = u[:, :, i]
        g_i = g[:, :, i]
        w_i = w[:, :, i]
        k_neg_i = k_neg[:, :, i]
        q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]

        Aqk = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, k_neg_i.transpose(-2, -1))
        Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_upper, 0.0)

        v_corrected = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S)
        o_i = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_corrected)
        o[:, :, i] = o_i

        ge = g_i[:, :, -1].exp()
        S = S * ge.unsqueeze(-1)
        gd = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
        S = S + torch.matmul((k_i * gd).transpose(-2, -1), v_corrected)

    o = rearrange(o, "b h n c d -> b (n c) h d")
    return o.to(dtype)


class Model(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, B: int, T: int, H: int, K: int, V: int, chunk_size: int = 64):
        super().__init__()
        self.B, self.T, self.H, self.K, self.V = B, T, H, K, V
        self.chunk_size = chunk_size
        self.scale = float(K) ** -0.5
        self.register_buffer("_dummy", torch.zeros(1), persistent=False)

    def forward(self, q, k, v, g, beta):
        return _kda_forward_pytorch(q, k, v, g, beta, scale=self.scale, chunk_size=self.chunk_size)


# Module-level shape shims
B = 2
T = 1024
H = 8
K = 128
V = 128
CHUNK_SIZE = 64


def get_inputs():
    torch.manual_seed(0)
    q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
    k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
    v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16) * 0.1
    g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32) * 0.1 - 0.05)
    beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
    return [q, k, v, g, beta]


def get_init_inputs():
    return [B, T, H, K, V, CHUNK_SIZE]

<content>
1: name: 02_kda_cutlass
2: display_name: "Kimi Delta Attention (chunk forward) via CUTLASS CuTe"
3: precision: bf16
4: regime: compute
5: 
6: # Approximate FLOPs per forward call. KDA forward (chunk form) breakdown per
7: # token across all heads:
8: #   - intra-chunk Aqk (q @ k.T with decay): 2*BT*K
9: #   - intra-chunk Akk + cumulative invert : ~3*BT*K + BT^2
10: #   - w = A @ (g.exp()*k):                  2*BT*K
11: #   - u = A @ v:                            2*BT*V
12: #   - inter-chunk q @ S:                    2*K*V
13: #   - inter-chunk (Aqk @ v_i):              2*BT*V
14: #   - state update S += k.T @ v_i:          2*K*V
15: # Aggregating with a constant of 4 (typical for chunked linear attention) gives
16: # the formula below. Used only for roofline reporting -- not graded directly.
17: flops_formula: "4 * B * T * H * (K*V + CHUNK_SIZE*K + CHUNK_SIZE*V)"
18: 
19: # Bytes moved (lower bound): one read of q,k,v,g,beta and one write of o.
20: bytes_formula: "B*T*H*K*2 + B*T*H*K*2 + B*T*H*V*2 + B*T*H*K*4 + B*T*H*2 + B*T*H*V*2"
21: 
22: hardware: [RTX_PRO_6000]
23: peak_tflops_key: bf16  # KDA's heavy work is bf16 @ bf16 -> fp32 GEMM-equivalent
24: peak_bandwidth_key: dram
25: 
26: # bf16 default tolerance from src/eval/correctness.py is 1e-2 atol/rtol; KDA's
27: # long recurrence accumulates more error than a single GEMM, so we relax slightly.
28: tolerance:
29:   torch.bfloat16: 0.0

2: 
3: Mix of:
4:   - short-context training-step scale (T=1024)
5:   - mid-context (T=2048) which is the headline benchmark
6:   - long-context that stresses the inter-chunk recurrence (T=4096)

8:

10:   - T % chunk_size == 0 (chunk_size = 64)

+"""KDA forward (chunk form) — custom CUDA implementation via `load_inline`.
+
+Uses CUDA C++ kernels compiled at runtime for the core operations:
+  • intra-chunk A matrix (k_neg_exp @ k_exp.T with lower-triangular masking)
+  • cumulative correction (forward substitution for (I−A)^{-1})
+  • w = A @ k_exp, u = A @ v
+  • inter-chunk recurrence (buffered state S)
+"""
+
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+from einops import rearrange
+from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline
+
+# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+# CUDA source  – a single fused kernel for all of KDA forward
+# ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+
+_cuda_src = r"""
+#include <cuda_runtime.h>
+#include <cuda_bf16.h>
+#include <cuda_fp16.h>
+
+using bf16 = __nv_bfloat16;
+
+// -----------------------------------------------------------------------
+// Helper: warp-level reduce sum of a float (across warp)
+// -----------------------------------------------------------------------
+__device__ __forceinline__ float warp_reduce_sum(float v) {
+    v += __shfl_xor_sync(0xffffffff, v, 16);
+    v += __shfl_xor_sync(0xffffffff, v, 8);
+    v += __shfl_xor_sync(0xffffffff, v, 4);
+    v += __shfl_xor_sync(0xffffffff, v, 2);
+    v += __shfl_xor_sync(0xffffffff, v, 1);
+    return v;
+}
+
+// -----------------------------------------------------------------------
+// Fused intra-chunk kernel: for each (b,h,n) compute A, w, u.
+//
+// Grid: (B * H * N)  blocks, each block handles one chunk.
+// Block: 128 threads (or more, tiled across C dimension).
+//
+// Inputs  (all already rearranged to chunk form (B,H,N,C,D)):
+//   k_ptr, g_ptr, beta_ptr, v_ptr  (strides: B,H,N,C,D order)
+// Outputs:
+//   w_ptr, u_ptr                   (strides: B,H,N,C,D)
+//   A_ptr (optional, for debugging)
+//
+// We compute in FP32 for accuracy and cast back to bf16 for output.
+// -----------------------------------------------------------------------
+
+constexpr int C = 64;   // chunk size (compile-time constant for this problem)
+constexpr int K = 128;  // key dim
+constexpr int V = 128;  // value dim
+
+// Strides for the 5D tensor (B,H,N,C,D) in elements, NOT bytes.
+// We compute strides from the tensor shape inside the kernel.
+// Since all tensors share B,H,N,C for the first 4 dims (except beta which lacks D),
+// we pass:
+//   stride_b = H*N*C*D
+//   stride_h = N*C*D
+//   stride_n = C*D
+//   stride_c = D
+//   stride_d = 1
+
+__global__ void intra_chunk_kernel(
+    const bf16* __restrict__ k_ptr,
+    const float* __restrict__ g_ptr,
+    const bf16* __restrict__ beta_ptr,
+    const bf16* __restrict__ v_ptr,
+    bf16* __restrict__ w_ptr,
+    bf16* __restrict__ u_ptr,
+    int B, int H, int N,
+    int stride_b_k, int stride_h_k, int stride_n_k, int stride_c_k, int stride_d_k,
+    int stride_b_g, int stride_h_g, int stride_n_g, int stride_c_g, int stride_d_g,
+    int stride_b_beta, int stride_h_beta, int stride_n_beta, int stride_c_beta,
+    int stride_b_v, int stride_h_v, int stride_n_v, int stride_c_v, int stride_d_v,
+    int stride_b_w, int stride_h_w, int stride_n_w, int stride_c_w, int stride_d_w,
+    int stride_b_u, int stride_h_u, int stride_n_u, int stride_c_u, int stride_d_u
+) {
+    // Block index = flat chunk index
+    int chunk_id = blockIdx.x;        // 0..B*H*N-1
+    int n = chunk_id % N;
+    int hn = chunk_id / N;
+    int h = hn % H;
+    int b = hn / H;
+
+    // Shared memory for A (CxC float) and temporary buffers
+    __shared__ float smem_A[C * C];        // A matrix (column-major: row-major with stride_C)
+    __shared__ float smem_k_exp[C * K];    // k * exp(g)  (row-major: [i][d])
+    __shared__ float smem_k_neg[C * K];    // k * exp(-g) (row-major: [j][d])
+    __shared__ float smem_v[C * V];        // v values
+    __shared__ float smem_beta[C];         // beta values
+
+    // Load k, g, beta, v for this chunk into shared memory
+    for (int idx = threadIdx.x; idx < C * K; idx += blockDim.x) {
+        int i = idx / K;
+        int d = idx % K;
+        int offset_k = b * stride_b_k + h * stride_h_k + n * stride_n_k + i * stride_c_k + d * stride_d_k;
+        k_ptr[offset_k]; // touch for pre-fetch? just load
+    }
+}
+""";
+
+
+# For simplicity, start with an efficient PyTorch implementation,
+# then layer on CUDA/Triton kernels incrementally.
+
+def _kda_forward_pytorch(
+    q: torch.Tensor,
+    k: torch.Tensor,
+    v: torch.Tensor,
+    g: torch.Tensor,
+    beta: torch.Tensor,
+    scale: float,
+    chunk_size: int = 64,
+) -> torch.Tensor:
+    """KDA forward using efficient PyTorch batch matmuls (no Python loops)."""
+    dtype = v.dtype
+    B, T, H, K_dim = q.shape
+    V_dim = v.shape[-1]
+    BT = chunk_size
+    NT = T // BT
+
+    q = q * scale
+    q, k, v, g, beta = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q, k, v, g, beta))
+
+    # Rearrange to chunk form
+    q = rearrange(q, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
+    k = rearrange(k, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
+    v = rearrange(v, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
+    g = rearrange(g, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
+    beta = rearrange(beta, "b (n c) h -> b h n c", c=BT)
+
+    # Intra-chunk cumsum of g
+    g = g.cumsum(-2)
+
+    # Precompute exponentials
+    k_exp = k * g.exp()            # (B, H, N, C, K)
+    k_neg_exp = k * (-g).exp()     # (B, H, N, C, K)
+    q_exp = q * g.exp()            # (B, H, N, C, K)
+
+    # ---- Build A matrix (batch matmul + mask + cumulative correction) ----
+    # A = k_neg_exp @ k_exp^T   (B, H, N, C, C)
+    A = torch.matmul(k_neg_exp, k_exp.transpose(-2, -1))
+
+    # A = A * beta[..., None]   beta: (B,H,N,C) -> (B,H,N,C,1) -> broadcast
+    A = A * beta.unsqueeze(-1)
+    # Zero upper triangle (including diag) and negate: A = -(A .* triu_mask)
+    mask_diag_upper = torch.triu(tor

... (3511 more chars)

import torch
import reference
import solution

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128

# Reference model
ref_model = reference.Model(B, T, H, K, V).to(device).eval()
sol_model = solution.Model(B, T, H, K, V).to(device).eval()

# Get inputs
torch.manual_seed(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) if hasattr(t, 'to') else t for t in reference.get_inputs()]

# Apply large_qkv stress (amplify inputs)
q, k, v, g, beta = base_inputs
scale = 3.0
q = q * scale
k = k * scale
v = v * scale
inputs = [q, k, v, g, beta]

with torch.no_grad():
    ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
    sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)

diff = (ref_out.float() - sol_out.float()).abs()
max_idx = diff.argmax().item()
print(f'Max diff: {diff.max().item():.6f}')
print(f'Max idx: {max_idx}')
print(f'Shape: {ref_out.shape}')
# Unravel index
idx_flat = max_idx
for dim in reversed(ref_out.shape):
    print(f'  dim {dim}: {idx_flat % dim}')
    idx_flat //= dim

# Compare at worst point
print(f'Ref at worst: {ref_out.flatten()[max_idx]}')
print(f'Sol at worst: {sol_out.flatten()[max_idx]}')

import torch
import reference
import solution

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128

# Run nominal first
torch.manual_seed(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) if hasattr(t, 'to') else t for t in reference.get_inputs()]

with torch.no_grad():
    ref_out = reference._naive_chunk_kda(*base_inputs, scale=K**-0.5, chunk_size=64)
    sol_out = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(base_inputs[0], base_inputs[1], base_inputs[2], base_inputs[3], base_inputs[4], scale=K**-0.5, chunk_size=64)

diff = (ref_out.float() - sol_out.float()).abs()
print(f'Nominal - Max diff: {diff.max().item():.6f}')
print(f'Nominal - Mean diff: {diff.mean().item():.6f}')
bad = (diff > 0.05).sum().item()
print(f'Bad entries (>0.05): {bad} / {diff.numel()}')
if bad > 0:
    print(f'Worst: {diff.max().item()}')
    
# Now try large_qkv (amplify by 3x)
q, k, v, g, beta = base_inputs
q = q * 3
k = k * 3
v = v * 3
inputs_large = [q, k, v, g, beta]

with torch.no_grad():
    ref_out_large = reference._naive_chunk_kda(*inputs_large, scale=K**-0.5, chunk_size=64)
    sol_out_large = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(*inputs_large, scale=K**-0.5, chunk_size=64)

diff_large = (ref_out_large.float() - sol_out_large.float()).abs()
print(f'Large_qkv - Max diff: {diff_large.max().item():.6f}')
print(f'Large_qkv - Mean diff: {diff_large.mean().item():.6f}')
bad_large = (diff_large > 0.05 * (ref_out_large.float().abs() + 1e-8)).sum().item()
print(f'Large_qkv - Bad entries: {bad_large} / {diff_large.numel()}')

def numeric_stress_cases(problem_name: str) -> tuple[NumericStressCase, ...]:
    if os.environ.get("KBH_NUMERIC_STRESS", "1").lower() in {"0", "false", "no"}:
        return (NOMINAL_CASE,)
    return (NOMINAL_CASE, *_CASES.get(problem_name, ()))

"""Numeric distribution stress cases for correctness checks.

These cases are not hidden shapes. They rerun the same shape/seed validation
under a few scale regimes that catch kernels that only work for the nominal
N(0, 1)-ish inputs.
"""
from __future__ import annotations

import os
from collections.abc import Iterator, Mapping, Sequence
from contextlib import contextmanager
from dataclasses import dataclass, field

import torch

ToleranceOverride = Mapping[str, float | Mapping[str, float]]


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class NumericStressCase:
    name: str
    input_scales: Mapping[int, float] = field(default_factory=dict)
    state_scales: Mapping[str, float] = field(default_factory=dict)
    tolerance: ToleranceOverride | None = None


NOMINAL_CASE = NumericStressCase("nominal")

_SMALL_BF16 = {"bfloat16": {"atol": 1e-4, "rtol": 5e-2}}
_MED_BF16 = {"bfloat16": {"atol": 5e-4, "rtol": 5e-2}}
_LARGE_BF16 = {"bfloat16": {"atol": 2e-1, "rtol": 5e-2}}
_TINY_FP32 = {"float32": {"atol": 1e-7, "rtol": 1e-4}}
_LARGE_FP32 = {"float32": {"atol": 1e-1, "rtol": 1e-4}}

_CASES: dict[str, tuple[NumericStressCase, ...]] = {
    "01_fp8_gemm": (
        NumericStressCase("small_input", input_scales={0: 1e-3}, tolerance=_SMALL_BF16),
        NumericStressCase("large_input", input_scales={0: 64.0}, tolerance=_LARGE_BF16),
        NumericStressCase(
            "small_weight",
            state_scales={"weight": 1e-2},
            tolerance=_SMALL_BF16,
        ),
    ),
    "02_kda_cutlass": (

import torch
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64
scale = K ** -0.5

torch.manual_seed(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

# Apply large_qkv scaling
q = q * 2
k = k * 2
v = v * 2

# Compute A using reference method for a single chunk (b=0, h=0, n=0)
q_f, k_f, v_f, g_f, beta_f = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q, k, v, g, beta))
q_f = q_f * scale

q_r = rearrange(q_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(k_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(v_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(g_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(beta_f, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)

g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

# Reference A computation for chunk (0,0,0)
k_chunk = k_r[0, 0, 0]  # (C, K)
g_chunk = g_r[0, 0, 0]  # (C, K)

A_ref = torch.zeros(BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for i in range(BT):
    k_i = k_chunk[i]  # (K,)
    g_i = g_chunk[i:i+1]  # (1, K)
    # A_ref[i, j] = sum_d k[j,d] * exp(g[j,d] - g[i,d]) * k[i,d]
    A_ref[:, i] = torch.einsum('c d, d -> c', k_chunk * (g_chunk - g_i).exp(), k_i)

# My computation
k_exp = k_chunk * g_chunk.exp()  # (C, K)
k_neg = k_chunk * (-g_chunk).exp()
A_mine = k_exp @ k_neg.T  # (C, C)

print(f'A_ref shape: {A_ref.shape}')
print(f'A_mine shape: {A_mine.shape}')
print(f'Max diff pre-mask: {(A_ref - A_mine).abs().max().item()}')

# Apply mask
A_ref_m = A_ref * beta_r[0,0,0,:,None]
A_ref_m = -torch.triu(A_ref_m, diagonal=0)

A_mine_m = A_mine * beta_r[0,0,0,:,None]
A_mine_m = -torch.triu(A_mine_m, diagonal=0)

print(f'Max diff post-mask: {(A_ref_m - A_mine_m).abs().max().item()}')

# Cumulative correction - compare
A_ref_c = A_ref_m.clone()
for i in range(1, BT):
    # A_ref_c[i, :i] = A_ref_c[i, :i] + sum_j A_ref_c[i,j] * A_ref_c[j,:i]
    A_ir = A_ref_c[i, :, None]  # (BT, 1)
    A_left = A_ref_c[:, :i]      # (BT, i)
    delta = (A_ir * A_left).sum(-2)  # (i,)
    A_ref_c[i, :i] = A_ref_c[i, :i] + delta

A_mine_c = A_mine_m.clone()
for i in range(1, BT):
    A_row = A_mine_c[i, :, None]  # (BT, 1)
    A_left = A_mine_c[:, :i]       # (BT, i)
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)  # (i,)
    A_mine_c[i, :i] = A_mine_c[i, :i] + delta

print(f'Max diff post-correction: {(A_ref_c - A_mine_c).abs().max().item()}')

# Check w and u
A_ref_final = (A_ref_c + torch.eye(BT, device=device)) * beta_r[0,0,0,:,None]
A_mine_final = (A_mine_c + torch.eye(BT, device=device)) * beta_r[0,0,0,:,None]

w_ref = A_ref_final @ k_exp
w_mine = A_mine_final @ k_exp
print(f'Max diff w: {(w_ref - w_mine).abs().max().item()}')

u_ref = A_ref_final @ v_r[0,0,0]
u_mine = A_mine_final @ v_r[0,0,0]
print(f'Max diff u: {(u_ref - u_mine).abs().max().item()}')

# Inter-chunk comparison for first chunk
S_ref = torch.zeros(K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
S_mine = torch.zeros(K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)

q_exp = q_r[0,0,0] * g_r[0,0,0].exp()  # (C, K)
k_neg = k_r[0,0,0] * (-g_r[0,0,0]).exp()  # (C, K)

# Aqk ref
Aqk_ref = torch.zeros(BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for j in range(BT):
    k_j = k_r[0,0,0,j]  # (K,)
    g_j = g_r[0,0,0,j:j+1]
    Aqk_ref[:, j] = torch.einsum('c d, d -> c', q_exp * (g_r[0,0,0] - g_j).exp(), k_j)
mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=1)
Aqk_ref = Aqk_ref.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)

# Aqk mine
Aqk_mine = q_exp @ k_neg.T
Aqk_mine = Aqk_mine.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)

print(f'Max diff Aqk: {(Aqk_ref - Aqk_mine).abs().max().item()}')
" 2>&1
tool

A_ref shape: torch.Size([64, 64])
A_mine shape: torch.Size([64, 64])
Max diff pre-mask: 0.010016918182373047
Max diff post-mask: 0.00696486234664917

import torch
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64
scale = K ** -0.5

torch.manual_seed(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

q = q * 2
k = k * 2
v = v * 2

q_f, k_f, v_f, g_f, beta_f = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q, k, v, g, beta))
q_f = q_f * scale

q_r = rearrange(q_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(k_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(v_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(g_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)

g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

q_chunk = q_r[0,0,0]  # (C, K)
k_chunk = k_r[0,0,0]  # (C, K)
g_chunk = g_r[0,0,0]  # (C, K)

# q_exp
q_exp = q_chunk * g_chunk.exp()  # (C, K)

# k_neg
k_neg = k_chunk * (-g_chunk).exp()  # (C, K)

# Aqk via matmul
Aqk_mm = q_exp @ k_neg.T

# Aqk via reference einsum
Aqk_ref = torch.zeros(BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for j in range(BT):
    k_j = k_chunk[j]
    g_j = g_chunk[j:j+1]
    Aqk_ref[:, j] = torch.einsum('c d, d -> c', q_exp * (g_chunk - g_j).exp(), k_j)

print(f'Max diff Aqk: {(Aqk_mm - Aqk_ref).abs().max().item()}')

# Also check: q_exp * (g_chunk - g_j).exp() should equal q_exp * exp(g) * exp(-g_j) = ...

for j in [0, 1, 2, 32, 63]:
    q_exp_g_diff = q_exp * (g_chunk - g_chunk[j:j+1]).exp()
    q_exp_k_neg = q_exp * (k_neg[j:j+1]).exp()  # This is wrong
    # Actually let me check: exp(g[c] - g[j]) = exp(g[c]) * exp(-g[j])
    # q_exp[c] = q[c] * exp(g[c])
    # q_exp[c] * exp(g[c] - g[j]) = q[c] * exp(g[c]) * exp(g[c] - g[j])
    #                              = q[c] * exp(2*g[c] - g[j])
    # Hmm, that's not right either.
    # q_exp[c] = q[c] * exp(g[c])
    # And the reference: sum_d q_exp[c,d] * exp(g[c,d] - g[j,d])... wait no
    # Aqk[c,j] = sum_d q_i[c,d] * exp(g_i[c,d] - g_j[d]) * k_j[d]
    #          = sum_d q[c,d] * exp(g[c,d]) * exp(g[c,d] - g[j,d]) * k[j,d]
    
# Let me just compute directly: 
# Aqk_ref[c,j] = sum_d q[c,d] * exp(g[c,d] - g[j,d]) * k[j,d]
# With scaling: q_actual[c,d] = q_orig[c,d] * scale
# Aqk_ref[c,j] = sum_d q_scale[c,d] * exp(g[c,d] - g[j,d]) * k[j,d]
Aqk_mm2 = torch.zeros(BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
# Compute as q_exp @ k_neg.T where q_exp = q * exp(g) but what about q * exp(g) in the ref?
# Aqk_ref uses q_i * (g_i - g_j).exp() * k_j
# = q * exp(g - g_j) * k_j
# = q * exp(g) * exp(-g_j) * k_j
# = (q * exp(g)) * (k_j * exp(-g_j))
# = q_exp[c] * k_neg[j]
# Aqk_mm2[c,j] = sum_d q_exp[c,d] * k_neg[j,d]
# So Aqk_mm2 = q_exp @ k_neg.T
# But sum_d q_exp[c,d] * k_neg.T[d,j] = sum_d q_exp[c,d] * k_neg[j,d]
# That's exactly q_exp @ k_neg.T

c_idx, j_idx = 5, 10
ref_val = torch.sum(q_exp[c_idx] * (g_chunk[c_idx] - g_chunk[j_idx]).exp() * k_chunk[j_idx])
mm_val = torch.sum(q_exp[c_idx] * k_neg[j_idx])

from einops import rearrange

k_in = k.clone()

    sol_o = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(q_in, k_in, v_in, g_in, beta_in, scale=K**-0.5, chunk_size=BT)

diff = (ref_o.float() - sol_o.float()).abs()
print(f'Nominal (no scaling) - Max abs diff: {diff.max().item():.6f}')
bad = (diff > 0.05).sum().item()
print(f'Bad entries: {bad} / {diff.numel()}')

v_in2 = v * 2
with torch.no_grad():
    ref_o2 = reference._naive_chunk_kda(q_in2, k_in2, v_in2, g_in2, beta_in, scale=K**-0.5, chunk_size=BT)
    sol_o2 = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(q_in2, k_in2, v_in2, g_in2, beta_in, scale=K**-0.5, chunk_size=BT)

bad2 = (diff2 > 0.05).sum().item()

print(f'Worst idx: {diff2.argmax().item()}')

# Check where the largest differences are

sorted_vals, sorted_idx = torch.sort(vals, descending=True)
print(f'Top 5 differences: {sorted_vals[:5]}')
for i in range(5):
    idx = sorted_idx[i].item()
    # unroll the index
    idx_c = idx % V
    idx_h = (idx // V) % H
    idx_t = (idx // (V * H)) % T
    idx_b = idx // (T * V * H)

import torch
import reference
import solution

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) if hasattr(t, 'to') else t for t in reference.get_inputs()]

# Apply large_qkv scaling
q, k, v, g, beta = base_inputs
scale_q = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
scale_k = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
scale_v = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

with torch.no_grad():
    ref_out = reference._naive_chunk_kda(scale_q, scale_k, scale_v, g, beta, scale=K**-0.5, chunk_size=64)
    sol_out = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(scale_q, scale_k, scale_v, g, beta, scale=K**-0.5, chunk_size=64)

diff = (ref_out.float() - sol_out.float()).abs()
ref_abs = ref_out.float().abs()

# Find entries where BOTH exceed tolerance
bad_mask = (diff > 0.05) & (diff > 0.05 * ref_abs)
print(f'Bad entries: {bad_mask.sum().item()}')

# Check the worst entries
worst_idx = diff.argmax().item()
b = worst_idx // (T * H * V)
t = (worst_idx // (H * V)) % T
h = (worst_idx // V) % H
v_idx = worst_idx % V
print(f'Worst: [{b},{t},{h},{v_idx}] diff={diff.flatten()[worst_idx].item():.6f} ref={ref_out.flatten()[worst_idx].item():.6f} sol={sol_out.flatten()[worst_idx].item():.6f}')

# Check if ref and sol differ in intermediate values
# Let's trace through the cumulative correction for specific (b,h) and a specific chunk
b_idx, h_idx = 0, 0

# Compute using my implementation step by step
import solution as sol_mod
q_f, k_f, v_f, g_f, beta_f = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (scale_q, scale_k, scale_v, g, beta))
q_f = q_f * (K ** -0.5)

from einops import rearrange
BT = 64
q_r = rearrange(q_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(k_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(v_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(g_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(beta_f, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
k_neg = k_r * (-g_r).exp()

A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A = -torch.triu(A, diagonal=0)

# My cumulative correction
A_sol = A.clone()
for i in range(1, BT):
    A_row = A_sol[..., i, :, None]
    A_left = A_sol[..., :, :i]
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
    A_sol[..., i, :i] = A_sol[..., i, :i] + delta

# Reference cumulative correction (with clone)
A_ref = A.clone()
for i in range(1, BT):
    A_ref[..., i, :i] = A_ref[..., i, :i].clone() + (A_ref[..., i, :, None].clone() * A_ref[..., :, :i].clone()).sum(-2)

diff_A = (A_sol - A_ref).abs()
print(f'Max diff in A after correction: {diff_A.max().item():.10f}')
print(f'Mean diff in A: {diff_A.mean().item():.10f}')

# Without clone() in reference - same as my code
A_ref2 = A.clone()
for i in range(1, BT):
    A_row2 = A_ref2[..., i, :, None]
    A_left2 = A_ref2[..., :, :i]
    delta2 = (A_row2 * A_left2).sum(-2)
    A_ref2[..., i, :i] = A_ref2[..., i, :i] + delta2

diff_A2 = (A_ref - A_ref2).abs()
print(f'Max diff in A (ref vs ref-no-clone): {diff_A2.max().item():.10f}')

import torch
import reference
import solution
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) if hasattr(t, 'to') else t for t in reference.get_inputs()]

q, k, v, g, beta = base_inputs
q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

# Build complete reference computation step by step
q_f, k_f, v_f, g_f, beta_f = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
scale = K ** -0.5
q_f = q_f * scale

q_r = rearrange(q_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(k_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(v_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(g_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(beta_f, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
k_neg = k_r * (-g_r).exp()
q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A = -torch.triu(A, diagonal=0)

for i in range(1, BT):
    A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i].clone() + (A[..., i, :, None].clone() * A[..., :, :i].clone()).sum(-2)

A = (A + torch.eye(BT, device=A.device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)

# Now inter-chunk - compare my implementation vs reference for each chunk
S_ref = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
S_mine = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)

mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=1)

for i in range(T // BT):
    q_i = q_r[:, :, i]
    q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, i]
    v_i_val = v_r[:, :, i]
    u_i = u[:, :, i]
    g_i = g_r[:, :, i]
    w_i = w[:, :, i]
    k_neg_i = k_neg[:, :, i]
    
    # Reference Aqk
    Aqk_ref = torch.zeros(B, H, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
    for j in range(BT):
        k_j = k_i[:, :, j, :]
        g_j = g_i[:, :, j:j+1, :]
        Aqk_ref[:, :, :, j] = torch.einsum('... c d, ... d -> ... c', q_i * (g_i - g_j).exp(), k_j)
    Aqk_ref = Aqk_ref.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
    
    # My Aqk
    Aqk_mine = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, k_neg_i.transpose(-2, -1))
    Aqk_mine = Aqk_mine.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
    
    diff_Aqk = (Aqk_ref - Aqk_mine).abs().max()
    
    # Reference v_i
    v_i_ref = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S_ref)
    v_i_mine = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S_mine)
    diff_v = (v_i_ref - v_i_mine).abs().max()
    
    # Reference o_i
    o_i_ref = torch.matmul(q_i * g_i.exp(), S_ref) + torch.matmul(Aqk_ref, v_i_ref)
    o_i_mine = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S_mine) + torch.matmul(Aqk_mine, v_i_mine)
    diff_o = (o_i_ref - o_i_mine).abs().max()
    
    if diff_o > 0.01:
        print(f'Chunk {i}: diff_Aqk={diff_Aqk:.10f} diff_v={diff_v:.10f} diff_o={diff_o:.10f}')
        print(f'  S_ref sample: {S_ref[0,0,:3,:3]}')
        print(f'  S_mine sample: {S_mine[0,0,:3,:3]}')
        diff_S = (S_ref - S_mine).abs().max()
        print(f'  diff_S: {diff_S:.10f}')
    
    # Update S - reference
    S_ref = S_ref * g_i[:, :, -1].exp().unsqueeze(-1)
    g_diff_ref = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
    k_corrected_ref = k_i * g_diff_ref
    S_ref = S_ref + torch.matmul(k_corrected_ref.transpose(-2, -1), v_i_ref)
    
    # Update S - mine (same as reference for comparison)
    S_mine = S_mine * g_i[:, :, -1].exp().unsqueeze(-1)
    g_diff_mine = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
    k_corrected_mine = k_i * g_diff_mine
    S_mine = S_mine + torch.matmul(k_corrected_mine.transpose(-2, -1), v_i_mine)

print('Done')
" 2>&1

import torch
import reference
import solution
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) if hasattr(t, 'to') else t for t in reference.get_inputs()]

q, k, v, g, beta = base_inputs
q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

q_f, k_f, v_f, g_f, beta_f = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
scale = K ** -0.5
q_f = q_f * scale

q_r = rearrange(q_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(k_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(v_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(g_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(beta_f, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
k_neg = k_r * (-g_r).exp()
q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A = -torch.triu(A, diagonal=0)

for i in range(1, BT):
    A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i].clone() + (A[..., i, :, None].clone() * A[..., :, :i].clone()).sum(-2)

A = (A + torch.eye(BT, device=A.device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)

S_ref = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
S_mine = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=1)
o_ref = torch.zeros_like(v_r)
o_mine = torch.zeros_like(v_r)

for i in range(T // BT):
    q_i = q_r[:, :, i]
    q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, i]
    u_i = u[:, :, i]
    g_i = g_r[:, :, i]
    w_i = w[:, :, i]
    k_neg_i = k_neg[:, :, i]
    
    # Aqk ref (uses plain q)
    Aqk_ref = torch.zeros(B, H, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
    for j in range(BT):
        k_j = k_i[:, :, j, :]
        g_j = g_i[:, :, j:j+1, :]
        Aqk_ref[:, :, :, j] = torch.einsum('... c d, ... d -> ... c', q_i * (g_i - g_j).exp(), k_j)
    Aqk_ref = Aqk_ref.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
    
    # Aqk mine (uses q_exp)
    Aqk_mine = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, k_neg_i.transpose(-2, -1))
    Aqk_mine = Aqk_mine.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
    
    # Reference
    v_i_ref = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S_ref)
    o_i_ref = torch.matmul(q_i * g_i.exp(), S_ref) + torch.matmul(Aqk_ref, v_i_ref)
    o_ref[:, :, i] = o_i_ref
    
    S_ref = S_ref * g_i[:, :, -1].exp().unsqueeze(-1)
    g_diff_ref = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
    S_ref = S_ref + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff_ref).transpose(-2, -1), v_i_ref)
    
    # Mine
    v_i_mine = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S_mine)
    o_i_mine = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S_mine) + torch.matmul(Aqk_mine, v_i_mine)
    o_mine[:, :, i] = o_i_mine
    
    S_mine = S_mine * g_i[:, :, -1].exp().unsqueeze(-1)
    g_diff_mine = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
    S_mine = S_mine + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff_mine).transpose(-2, -1), v_i_mine)
    
    diff_Aqk = (Aqk_ref - Aqk_mine).abs().max()
    diff_v = (v_i_ref - v_i_mine).abs().max()
    diff_o = (o_i_ref - o_i_mine).abs().max()
    diff_S = (S_ref - S_mine).abs().max()
    print(f'Chunk {i}: diff_Aqk={diff_Aqk:.8f} diff_v={diff_v:.8f} diff_o={diff_o:.8f} diff_S={diff_S:.8f}')
    
    if diff_o > 0.001:
        print(f'  BREAKING at chunk {i}!')

o_ref_flat = rearrange(o_ref, 'b h n c d -> b (n c) h d')
o_mine_flat = rearrange(o_mine, 'b h n c d -> b (n c) h d')
diff_total = (o_ref_flat - o_mine_flat).abs()
print(f'Total max diff: {diff_total.max():.6f}')

import torch
import reference
import solution
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) if hasattr(t, 'to') else t for t in reference.get_inputs()]

q, k, v, g, beta = base_inputs
q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

# Run full solution
with torch.no_grad():
    full_out = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=K**-0.5, chunk_size=BT)

# Now run step-by-step (same as solution code)
q_f, k_f, v_f, g_f, beta_f = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
q_f = q_f * (K ** -0.5)

q_r = rearrange(q_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(k_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(v_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(g_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(beta_f, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
k_neg = k_r * (-g_r).exp()
q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A = -torch.triu(A, diagonal=0)

for i in range(1, BT):
    A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i].clone() + (A[..., i, :, None].clone() * A[..., :, :i].clone()).sum(-2)

A = (A + torch.eye(BT, device=A.device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)

S = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
o = torch.zeros_like(v_r)
mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=1)

for i in range(T // BT):
    q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, i]
    u_i = u[:, :, i]
    g_i = g_r[:, :, i]
    w_i = w[:, :, i]
    k_neg_i = k_neg[:, :, i]
    
    Aqk = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, k_neg_i.transpose(-2, -1))
    Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
    
    v_corrected = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S)
    o_i = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_corrected)
    o[:, :, i] = o_i
    
    g_exp_last = g_i[:, :, -1].exp()
    S = S * g_exp_last.unsqueeze(-1)
    g_diff = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
    S = S + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff).transpose(-2, -1), v_corrected)

o_step = rearrange(o, 'b h n c d -> b (n c) h d')

diff = (full_out - o_step).abs()
print(f'Max diff between full solution and step-by-step: {diff.max():.6f}')
print(f'Match: {(full_out == o_step).all().item()}')

import torch
import solution
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) if hasattr(t, 'to') else t for t in solution.get_inputs()]

q, k, v, g, beta = base_inputs
q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

# Run solution function
with torch.no_grad():
    out = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=K**-0.5, chunk_size=BT)

# Now reproduce all steps identically
q_f, k_f, v_f, g_f, beta_f = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
q_f = q_f * (K ** -0.5)

q_r = rearrange(q_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(k_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(v_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(g_f, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(beta_f, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)

print('After rearrange:')
print(f'  q_r shape: {q_r.shape}')
print(f'  k_r shape: {k_r.shape}')
print(f'  v_r shape: {v_r.shape}')
print(f'  g_r shape: {g_r.shape}')
print(f'  beta_r shape: {beta_r.shape}')

g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
k_neg = k_r * (-g_r).exp()
q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

# Solution's cumulative correction (without clone)
A_sol = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
A_sol = A_sol * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A_sol = -torch.triu(A_sol, diagonal=0)

for i in range(1, BT):
    A_row = A_sol[..., i, :, None]
    A_left = A_sol[..., :, :i]
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
    A_sol[..., i, :i] = A_sol[..., i, :i] + delta

# Step-by-step cumulative correction (with clone)
A_ste = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
A_ste = A_ste * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A_ste = -torch.triu(A_ste, diagonal=0)

for i in range(1, BT):
    A_ste[..., i, :i] = A_ste[..., i, :i].clone() + (A_ste[..., i, :, None].clone() * A_ste[..., :, :i].clone()).sum(-2)

diff_A = (A_sol - A_ste).abs()
print(f'Max diff in A between sol and step: {diff_A.max():.10f}')

# Check the rest
A = A_sol.clone()  # Use the no-clone version
A = (A + torch.eye(BT, device=A.device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)

S = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
o = torch.zeros_like(v_r)
mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=1)

for i in range(T // BT):
    q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, i]
    u_i = u[:, :, i]
    g_i = g_r[:, :, i]
    w_i = w[:, :, i]
    k_neg_i = k_neg[:, :, i]
    
    Aqk = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, k_neg_i.transpose(-2, -1))
    Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
    
    v_corrected = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S)
    o_i = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_corrected)
    o[:, :, i] = o_i
    
    g_exp_last = g_i[:, :, -1].exp()
    S = S * g_exp_last.unsqueeze(-1)
    g_diff = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
    S = S + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff).transpose(-2, -1), v_corrected)

o_ste = rearrange(o, 'b h n c d -> b (n c) h d')

diff = (out - o_ste).abs()
print(f'Max diff between full and step-by-step output: {diff.max():.6f}')

import torch
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)

# Recreate inputs exactly
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

# === Solution function path === 
dtype = v2.dtype
B_val, T_val, H_val, K_dim = q2.shape
V_dim = v2.shape[-1]
BT_val = 64
NT = T_val // BT_val
scale = float(K_dim) ** -0.5

qf, kf, vf, gf, betaf = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
qf = qf * scale

q_r = rearrange(qf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
k_r = rearrange(kf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
v_r = rearrange(vf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
g_r = rearrange(gf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
beta_r = rearrange(betaf, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT_val)

# === Critical: check beta values ===
print(f'beta_r shape: {beta_r.shape}')
print(f'beta_r dtype: {beta_r.dtype}')
print(f'beta_r[0,0,0,:5]: {beta_r[0,0,0,:5]}')

g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
k_neg = k_r * (-g_r).exp()
q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

# Build A (same as solution)
A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A = -torch.triu(A, diagonal=0)

for i in range(1, BT_val):
    A_row = A[..., i, :, None]
    A_left = A[..., :, :i]
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
    A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i] + delta

A = (A + torch.eye(BT_val, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)

w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)

S = torch.zeros(B_val, H_val, K_dim, V_dim, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
o = torch.zeros_like(v_r)

mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT_val, BT_val, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=1)

for i in range(NT):
    q_i = q_r[:, :, i]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, i]
    u_i = u[:, :, i]
    g_i = g_r[:, :, i]
    w_i = w[:, :, i]
    k_neg_i = k_neg[:, :, i]
    q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]

    Aqk = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, k_neg_i.transpose(-2, -1))
    Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)

    v_corrected = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S)
    o_i = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_corrected)
    o[:, :, i] = o_i

    # State update - check this carefully
    g_exp_last = g_i[:, :, -1].exp()
    S = S * g_exp_last.unsqueeze(-1)
    g_diff = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
    k_cor = k_i * g_diff
    S = S + torch.matmul((k_cor).transpose(-2, -1), v_corrected)

    if i == 0:
        print(f'Chunk 0: g_i[:,:,-1].exp() sample: {g_exp_last[0,0,:5]}')
        print(f'  g_diff sample: {g_diff[0,0,0,:5]}')
        print(f'  k_cor sample: {k_cor[0,0,0,:5]}')
        print(f'  S after: {S[0,0,:3,:3]}')

o_manual = rearrange(o, 'b h n c d -> b (n c) h d')

# === What does the actual solution function compute? ===
import solution
with torch.no_grad():
    o_sol = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=scale, chunk_size=BT_val)

diff = (o_manual - o_sol).abs()
print(f'Max diff manual vs solution: {diff.max():.6f}')

import torch
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

# === Step by step, injecting into solution function ===
import solution
# Let's add breakpoints by monkey-patching
orig_fn = solution._kda_forward_pytorch

# Create a test version with extra instrumentation
def _kda_forward_pytorch_instrumented(
    q, k, v, g, beta, scale, chunk_size=64
):
    dtype = v.dtype
    B, T, H, K_dim = q.shape
    V_dim = v.shape[-1]
    BT = chunk_size
    NT = T // BT

    q, k, v, g, beta = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q, k, v, g, beta))
    q = q * scale

    q = rearrange(q, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
    k = rearrange(k, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
    v = rearrange(v, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
    g = rearrange(g, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
    beta = rearrange(beta, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)

    g = g.cumsum(-2)
    k_exp = k * g.exp()
    k_neg_exp = k * (-g).exp()
    q_exp = q * g.exp()

    A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg_exp.transpose(-2, -1))
    A = A * beta.unsqueeze(-1)
    A = -torch.triu(A, diagonal=0)

    for i in range(1, BT):
        A_row = A[..., i, :, None]
        A_left = A[..., :, :i]
        delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
        A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i] + delta

    A = (A + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)) * beta.unsqueeze(-1)

    w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
    u = torch.matmul(A, v)

    S = torch.zeros(B, H, K_dim, V_dim, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)
    o = torch.zeros_like(v)

    mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=A.device), diagonal=1)

    for i in range(NT):
        q_i = q[:, :, i]
        k_i = k[:, :, i]
        u_i = u[:, :, i]
        g_i = g[:, :, i]
        w_i = w[:, :, i]
        k_neg_i = k_neg_exp[:, :, i]
        q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]

        Aqk_clone = torch.matmul(q_exp_i.clone(), k_neg_i.clone().transpose(-2, -1))
        Aqk_clone = Aqk_clone.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)

        Aqk = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, k_neg_i.transpose(-2, -1))
        Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)

        if i == 0:
            print(f'  Aqk eq: {(Aqk == Aqk_clone).all().item()}')            
            print(f'  Aqk max diff: {(Aqk - Aqk_clone).abs().max().item()}')

        v_corrected = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S)
        o_i = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_corrected)
        o[:, :, i] = o_i

        g_exp_last = g_i[:, :, -1].exp()
        S = S * g_exp_last.unsqueeze(-1)
        g_diff = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
        S = S + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff).transpose(-2, -1), v_corrected)

    o = rearrange(o, 'b h n c d -> b (n c) h d')
    return o.to(dtype)

with torch.no_grad():
    o1 = orig_fn(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=float(K)**-0.5, chunk_size=64)
    o2 = _kda_forward_pytorch_instrumented(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=float(K)**-0.5, chunk_size=64)

diff = (o1 - o2).abs()
print(f'Max diff between orig and instrumented: {diff.max():.6f}')
" 2>&1

  Aqk max diff: 0.0

import torch
from einops import rearrange
import solution

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

# Call the function directly
with torch.no_grad():
    out_direct = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=float(K)**-0.5, chunk_size=64)

# Now call same code but with explicit steps
dtype = v2.dtype
scale = float(K) ** -0.5
qf, kf, vf, gf, betaf = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
qf = qf * scale

q_r = rearrange(qf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(kf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(vf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(gf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(betaf, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)

g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)
k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
k_neg = k_r * (-g_r).exp()
q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A = -torch.triu(A, diagonal=0)
for i in range(1, BT):
    A_row = A[..., i, :, None]
    A_left = A[..., :, :i]
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
    A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i] + delta

A = (A + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)

S = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
o = torch.zeros_like(v_r)
mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=1)

for i in range(T // BT):
    q_i = q_r[:, :, i]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, i]
    u_i = u[:, :, i]
    g_i = g_r[:, :, i]
    w_i = w[:, :, i]
    k_neg_i = k_neg[:, :, i]
    q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]

    Aqk = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, k_neg_i.transpose(-2, -1))
    Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)

    v_corrected = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S)
    o_i = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_corrected)
    o[:, :, i] = o_i

    g_exp_last = g_i[:, :, -1].exp()
    S = S * g_exp_last.unsqueeze(-1)
    g_diff = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
    S = S + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff).transpose(-2, -1), v_corrected)

o_manual = rearrange(o, 'b h n c d -> b (n c) h d')
o_manual = o_manual.to(dtype)

diff = (out_direct - o_manual).abs()
print(f'Max diff: {diff.max():.6f}')

# Check specific positions
print(f'Sample manual: {o_manual[0,0,0,:5]}')
print(f'Sample direct: {out_direct[0,0,0,:5]}')

def _kda_forward_debug(q, k, v, g, beta, scale, chunk_size=64):
    dtype = v.dtype
    B, T, H, K_dim = q.shape
    V_dim = v.shape[-1]
    BT = chunk_size
    NT = T // BT

    q, k, v, g, beta = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q, k, v, g, beta))

    v_r = rearrange(v, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
    g_r = rearrange(g, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
    beta_r = rearrange(beta, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)

    g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)
    k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
    k_neg = k_r * (-g_r).exp()
    q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

    A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
    A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
    A = -torch.triu(A, diagonal=0)

    for i in range(1, BT):
        A_row = A[..., i, :, None]
        A_left = A[..., :, :i]
        delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
        A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i] + delta

    A = (A + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)

    v_corrected = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S)
    o_i = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_corrected)
    o[:, :, i] = o_i

    g_exp_last = g_i[:, :, -1].exp()
    S = S * g_exp_last.unsqueeze(-1)
    g_diff = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
    S = S + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff).transpose(-2, -1), v_corrected)

o_manual = rearrange(o, 'b h n c d -> b (n c) h d')
o_manual = o_manual.to(dtype)

diff = (out_fn - o_manual).abs()
print(f'Max diff: {diff.max():.6f}')
print(f'Sample fn: {out_fn[0,0,:5]}')
print(f'Sample manual: {o_manual[0,0,:5]}')

# Also check that q2 etc. are not modified
print(f'q2 unchanged: {q2[0,0,:5]}')

import torch
from einops import rearrange
import solution as sol_mod

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

# Step 1: Call the function and check its return
# Actually, let me just WRITE the function inline here to compare

scale = float(K) ** -0.5

# ====== Function code (copy-pasted) ======
dtype = v2.dtype
B_val, T_val, H_val, K_dim = q2.shape
V_dim = v2.shape[-1]
BT_val = 64
NT = T_val // BT_val

qf, kf, vf, gf, betaf = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
qf = qf * scale

q_r = rearrange(qf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
k_r = rearrange(kf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
v_r = rearrange(vf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
g_r = rearrange(gf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
beta_r = rearrange(betaf, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT_val)

g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)
k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
k_neg = k_r * (-g_r).exp()
q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A = -torch.triu(A, diagonal=0)
for i in range(1, BT_val):
    A_row = A[..., i, :, None]
    A_left = A[..., :, :i]
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
    A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i] + delta

A = (A + torch.eye(BT_val, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)

# We can't access the function's internal variables, but we can verify by
# comparing with the reference output

    o_ref = reference._naive_chunk_kda(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=scale, chunk_size=64)
    o_fn = sol_mod._kda_forward_pytorch(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=scale, chunk_size=64)

S = torch.zeros(B_val, H_val, K_dim, V_dim, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)
o_manual = torch.zeros_like(v_r)
mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT_val, BT_val, dtype=torch.bool, device=A.device), diagonal=1)

for i in range(NT):
    q_i = q_r[:, :, i]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, i]
    u_i = u[:, :, i]
    g_i = g_r[:, :, i]
    w_i = w[:, :, i]
    k_neg_i = k_neg[:, :, i]
    q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]

    Aqk = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, k_neg_i.transpose(-2, -1))
    Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
    v_corrected = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S)
    o_i = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_corrected)
    o_manual[:, :, i] = o_i

    g_exp_last = g_i[:, :, -1].exp()
    S = S * g_exp_last.unsqueeze(-1)
    g_diff = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
    S = S + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff).transpose(-2, -1), v_corrected)

o_manual_flat = rearrange(o_manual, 'b h n c d -> b (n c) h d')
o_manual_flat = o_manual_flat.to(dtype)

diff_manual_fn = (o_manual_flat.float() - o_fn.float()).abs().max()
print(f'Max diff manual vs function: {diff_manual_fn:.6f}')

diff_manual_ref = (o_manual_flat.float() - o_ref.float()).abs().max()

+"""Debug version - copies solution code exactly."""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+from einops import rearrange
+
+
+def _kda_forward_pytorch(
+    q: torch.Tensor,
+    k: torch.Tensor,
+    v: torch.Tensor,
+    g: torch.Tensor,
+    beta: torch.Tensor,
+    scale: float,
+    chunk_size: int = 64,
+) -> torch.Tensor:
+    dtype = v.dtype
+    B, T, H, K_dim = q.shape
+    V_dim = v.shape[-1]
+    BT = chunk_size
+    NT = T // BT
+
+    q, k, v, g, beta = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q, k, v, g, beta))
+    q = q * scale
+
+    q = rearrange(q, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
+    k = rearrange(k, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
+    v = rearrange(v, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
+    g = rearrange(g, "b (n c) h d -> b h n c d", c=BT)
+    beta = rearrange(beta, "b (n c) h -> b h n c", c=BT)
+
+    g = g.cumsum(-2)
+
+    k_exp = k * g.exp()
+    k_neg_exp = k * (-g).exp()
+    q_exp = q * g.exp()
+
+    A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg_exp.transpose(-2, -1))
+    A = A * beta.unsqueeze(-1)
+    A = -torch.triu(A, diagonal=0)
+
+    for i in range(1, BT):
+        A_row = A[..., i, :, None]
+        A_left = A[..., :, :i]
+        delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
+        A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i] + delta
+
+    A = (A + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)) * beta.unsqueeze(-1)
+
+    w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
+    u = torch.matmul(A, v)
+
+    S = torch.zeros(B, H, K_dim, V_dim, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)
+    o = torch.zeros_like(v)
+
+    mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=A.device), diagonal=1)
+
+    for i in range(NT):
+        q_i = q[:, :, i]
+        k_i = k[:, :, i]
+        u_i = u[:, :, i]
+        g_i = g[:, :, i]
+        w_i = w[:, :, i]
+        k_neg_i = k_neg_exp[:, :, i]
+        q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]
+
+        Aqk = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, k_neg_i.transpose(-2, -1))
+        Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
+
+        v_corrected = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S)
+        o_i = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_corrected)
+        o[:, :, i] = o_i
+
+        g_exp_last = g_i[:, :, -1].exp()
+        S = S * g_exp_last.unsqueeze(-1)
+        g_diff = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
+        S = S + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff).transpose(-2, -1), v_corrected)
+
+    o = rearrange(o, "b h n c d -> b (n c) h d")
+    return o.to(dtype)

< Uses CUDA C++ kernels compiled at runtime for the core operations:
<   • intra-chunk A matrix (k_neg_exp @ k_exp.T with lower-triangular masking)
<   • cumulative correction (forward substitution for (I−A)^{-1})
<   • w = A @ k_exp, u = A @ v
<   • inter-chunk recurrence (buffered state S)

< __device__ __forceinline__ float warp_reduce_sum(float v) {
<     v += __shfl_xor_sync(0xffffffff, v, 16);

<     v += __shfl_xor_sync(0xffffffff, v, 2);

args

  "description": "Check A matrix diff for large_qkv",

uv run python -c "
import torch
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

# 2x scaling
q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

scale = float(K) ** -0.5

# Reference A for first chunk (b=0,h=0,n=0)
qf, kf, vf, gf, betaf = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
qf = qf * scale

q_r = rearrange(qf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(kf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(vf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(gf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(betaf, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

# My A computation
k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
k_neg = k_r * (-g_r).exp()
A_mine = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))

# Reference A for first chunk
k_chunk = k_r[0,0,0]
g_chunk = g_r[0,0,0]
beta_chunk = beta_r[0,0,0]
A_ref = torch.zeros(BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for i in range(BT):
    k_i = k_chunk[i]
    g_i = g_chunk[i:i+1]
    A_ref[:, i] = torch.einsum('c d, d -> c', k_chunk * (g_chunk - g_i).exp(), k_i)

# Both un-masked
print(f'Max diff A (no mask): {(A_mine[0,0,0] - A_ref).abs().max():.10f}')

# Apply mask
A_ref_m = A_ref * beta_chunk[:, None]
A_ref_m = -A_ref_m.masked_fill(torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=0), 0.0)

A_mine_m = A_mine[0,0,0] * beta_chunk[:, None]
mask_diag_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=0)
A_mine_m = -A_mine_m.masked_fill(mask_diag_upper, 0.0)

print(f'Max diff A (masked): {(A_mine_m - A_ref_m).abs().max():.10f}')

# Cumulative correction
A_ref_c = A_ref_m.clone()
for i in range(1, BT):
    A_ref_c[i, :i] = A_ref_c[i, :i].clone() + (A_ref_c[i, :, None].clone() * A_ref_c[:, :i].clone()).sum(-2)

A_mine_c = A_mine_m.clone()
for i in range(1, BT):
    A_row = A_mine_c[i, :, None]
    A_left = A_mine_c[:, :i]
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
    A_mine_c[i, :i] = A_mine_c[i, :i] + delta

print(f'Max diff A (corrected): {(A_mine_c - A_ref_c).abs().max():.10f}')

# After adding I and beta multiply
A_ref_f = (A_ref_c + torch.eye(BT, device=device)) * beta_chunk[:, None]
A_mine_f = (A_mine_c + torch.eye(BT, device=device)) * beta_chunk[:, None]
print(f'Max diff A (final): {(A_mine_f - A_ref_f).abs().max():.10f}')

import torch
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

scale = float(K) ** -0.5
qf, kf, vf, gf, betaf = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
qf = qf * scale

q_r = rearrange(qf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(kf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(vf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(gf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(betaf, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
k_neg = k_r * (-g_r).exp()

A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg.transpose(-2, -1))
print(f'A range before mask: [{A.min().item():.6f}, {A.max().item():.6f}]')
A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
print(f'A range after beta: [{A.min().item():.6f}, {A.max().item():.6f}]')
A = -A.masked_fill(torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=A.device), diagonal=0), 0.0)
print(f'A range after mask: [{A.min().item():.6f}, {A.max().item():.6f}]')

for i in range(1, BT):
    A_row = A[..., i, :, None]
    A_left = A[..., :, :i]
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
    A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i] + delta

print(f'A range after correction: [{A.min().item():.6f}, {A.max().item():.6f}]')

A = (A + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
print(f'A range after final: [{A.min().item():.6f}, {A.max().item():.6f}]')

# Check w and u
w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)
print(f'w range: [{w.min().item():.6f}, {w.max().item():.6f}]')
print(f'u range: [{u.min().item():.6f}, {u.max().item():.6f}]')

# Check k_exp, k_neg
print(f'k_exp range: [{k_exp.min().item():.6f}, {k_exp.max().item():.6f}]')
print(f'g range: [{g_r.min().item():.6f}, {g_r.max().item():.6f}]')

    # Precompute exponentials
    k_exp = k * g.exp()            # (B, H, N, C, K)
    k_neg_exp = k * (-g).exp()     # (B, H, N, C, K)
    q_exp = q * g.exp()            # (B, H, N, C, K)

    # ---- Build A matrix (batch matmul + mask + cumulative correction) ----
    # A[c,i] = sum_d k[c,d] * exp(g[c,d] - g[i,d]) * k[i,d]
    #        = sum_d k_exp[c,d] * k_neg_exp[i,d]
    #        = k_exp @ k_neg_exp^T   (B, H, N, C, C)
    A = torch.matmul(k_exp, k_neg_exp.transpose(-2, -1))

    # A = A * beta[..., None]   beta: (B,H,N,C) -> (B,H,N,C,1) -> broadcast
    A = A * beta.unsqueeze(-1)
    # Zero upper triangle (including diag) and negate: A = -(A .* triu_mask)
    mask_diag_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=A.device), diagonal=0)
    A = -A.masked_fill(mask_diag_upper, 0.0)

    # Cumulative correction: (I - A)^{-1} - I, computed row by row
    # R[i, :i] = A[i, :i] + A[i, :] @ R[:, :i]
    for i in range(1, BT):
        A_row = A[..., i, :, None]   # (..., BT, 1) — row i as column vector
        A_left = A[..., :, :i]        # (..., BT, i) — first i columns
        delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)  # (..., i) = sum over BT dim
        A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i] + delta

    # A = (A + I) * beta[..., None, :]
    A = (A + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)) * beta.unsqueeze(-1)

    # ---- Compute w and u ----
    w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)  # (B, H, N, C, K)  --  w = A @ k_exp
    u = torch.matmul(A, v)      # (B, H, N, C, V)  --  u = A @ v

    # ---- Inter-chunk recurrence ----
    S = torch.zeros(B, H, K_dim, V_dim, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)
    o = torch.zeros_like(v)

    mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=A.device), diagonal=1)

    for i in range(NT):
        q_i = q[:, :, i]            # (B, H, C, K)
        k_i = k[:, :, i]            # (B, H, C, K)
        u_i = u[:, :, i]            # (B, H, C, V)
        g_i = g[:, :, i]            # (B, H, C, K)
        w_i = w[:, :, i]            # (B, H, C, K)
        k_neg_i = k_neg_exp[:, :, i]  # (B, H, C, K)
        q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]    # (B, H, C, K) — q * exp(g)

        # Aqk[c,j] = sum_d q[c,d] * exp(g[c,d] - g[j,d]) * k[j,d]
        # = sum_d q_exp[c,d] * k_neg[j,d] = q_exp @ k_neg.T
        Aqk = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, k_neg_i.transpose(-2, -1))
        Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)

        # v_corrected = u_i - w_i @ S
        v_corrected = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S)  # (B, H, C, V)
        o_i = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_corrected)  # (B, H, C, V)
        o[:, :, i] = o_i

        # State update
        g_exp_last = g_i[:, :, -1].exp()  # (B, H, K)
        S = S * g_exp_last.unsqueeze(-1)  # (B, H, K, V) * (B, H, K, 1)
        g_diff = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()  # (B, H, C, K)
        S = S + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff).transpose(-2, -1), v_corrected)
        # (K, C) @ (C, V) -> (K, V)

    # Precompute exponentials
    k_exp = k * g.exp()            # (B, H, N, C, K)
    q_exp = q * g.exp()            # (B, H, N, C, K)

    # ---- Build A matrix (batched per-column einsum matching reference) ----
    # A[c,i] = sum_d k[c,d] * exp(g[c,d] - g[i,d]) * k[i,d]
    # Compute column-by-column for numerical stability (matches reference exactly)
    A = torch.empty(B, H, NT, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=k.device)
    for i in range(BT):
        g_i = g[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]  # (B, H, N, 1, K)
        k_i = k[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]  # (B, H, N, 1, K)
        A[..., i] = (k * (g - g_i).exp() * k_i).sum(-1).squeeze(-1)  # (B, H, N, C)

    A = A * beta.unsqueeze(-1)
    mask_diag_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=A.device), diagonal=0)
    A = -A.masked_fill(mask_diag_upper, 0.0)

    # Cumulative correction: (I - A)^{-1} - I, computed row by row
    for i in range(1, BT):
        A_row = A[..., i, :, None]
        A_left = A[..., :, :i]
        delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
        A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i] + delta

    A = (A + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)) * beta.unsqueeze(-1)

    # ---- Compute w and u ----
    w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
    u = torch.matmul(A, v)

    # ---- Inter-chunk recurrence ----
    S = torch.zeros(B, H, K_dim, V_dim, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)

        w_i = w[:, :, i]

        Aqk = torch.empty(B, H, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=k.device)

            Aqk[..., j] = (q_i * (g_i - g_j).exp() * k_j).sum(-1).squeeze(-1)

import torch
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

scale = float(K) ** -0.5
qf, kf, vf, gf, betaf = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
qf = qf * scale

k_r = rearrange(kf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(gf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

# Reference A
k_chunk = k_r[0,0,0]
g_chunk = g_r[0,0,0]
A_ref = torch.zeros(BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for i in range(BT):
    k_i = k_chunk[i]
    g_i = g_chunk[i:i+1]
    A_ref[:, i] = torch.einsum('c d, d -> c', k_chunk * (g_chunk - g_i).exp(), k_i)

# My new A (batched column-by-column)
A_mine = torch.zeros(BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for i in range(BT):
    g_i = g_chunk[i:i+1]
    k_i = k_chunk[i:i+1]
    A_mine[:, i] = (k_chunk * (g_chunk - g_i).exp() * k_i).sum(-1).squeeze(-1)

print(f'Max diff A: {(A_ref - A_mine).abs().max():.10f}')

# Now compute full pipeline and compare with solution
import solution
with torch.no_grad():
    o_sol = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=scale, chunk_size=64)

import reference
with torch.no_grad():
    o_ref_fn = reference._naive_chunk_kda(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=scale, chunk_size=64)

diff = (o_ref_fn.float() - o_sol.float()).abs()
print(f'Max diff ref vs sol: {diff.max():.6f}')

from einops import rearrange
import reference, solution

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128

k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

    g_i = g_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    A[..., i] = (k_r * (g_r - g_i).exp() * k_i).sum(-1).squeeze(-1)

A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
mask_diag_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=0)
A = -A.masked_fill(mask_diag_upper, 0.0)

# Cumulative correction WITH clone (reference)
for i in range(1, BT):
    A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i].clone() + (A[..., i, :, None].clone() * A[..., :, :i].clone()).sum(-2)

A = (A + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)

# === Solution path ===
A2 = torch.zeros(B, H, T//BT, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for i in range(BT):
    g_i = g_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    A2[..., i] = (k_r * (g_r - g_i).exp() * k_i).sum(-1).squeeze(-1)

A2 = A2 * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A2 = -A2.masked_fill(mask_diag_upper, 0.0)

# Cumulative correction WITHOUT clone (my solution)
for i in range(1, BT):
    A_row = A2[..., i, :, None]
    A_left = A2[..., :, :i]
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
    A2[..., i, :i] = A2[..., i, :i] + delta

A2 = (A2 + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
w2 = torch.matmul(A2, k_exp)
u2 = torch.matmul(A2, v_r)

print(f'A max diff (ref vs sol): {(A - A2).abs().max():.10f}')
print(f'w max diff: {(w - w2).abs().max():.10f}')
print(f'u max diff: {(u - u2).abs().max():.10f}')

# Now check inter-chunk
S = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
S2 = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
o = torch.zeros_like(v_r)
o2 = torch.zeros_like(v_r)
mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=1)

NT = T // BT
for i in range(NT):
    q_i = q_r[:, :, i]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, i]
    u_i = u[:, :, i]
    g_i = g_r[:, :, i]
    w_i = w[:, :, i]
    q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]
    
    u_i2 = u2[:, :, i]
    w_i2 = w2[:, :, i]
    
    # Aqk ref
    Aqk = torch.zeros(B, H, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
    for j in range(BT):
        g_j = g_i[:, :, j:j+1, :]
        k_j = k_i[:, :, j:j+1, :]
        Aqk[..., j] = (q_i * (g_i - g_j).exp() * k_j).sum(-1).squeeze(-1)
    Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
    
    # Aqk sol
    Aqk2 = torch.zeros(B, H, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
    for j in range(BT):
        g_j = g_i[:, :, j:j+1, :]
        k_j = k_i[:, :, j:j+1, :]

    Aqk2 = Aqk2.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
    
    v_i = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S)
    o_i = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_i)
    o[:, :, i] =

import torch
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

scale = float(K) ** -0.5

# ---- This is exactly what the SOL file does (copy-pasted) ----
dtype = v2.dtype
B_val, T_val, H_val, K_dim = q2.shape
V_dim = v2.shape[-1]
BT_val = 64
NT = T_val // BT_val

qf, kf, vf, gf, betaf = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
qf = qf * scale

q_r = rearrange(qf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
k_r = rearrange(kf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
v_r = rearrange(vf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
g_r = rearrange(gf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT_val)
beta_r = rearrange(betaf, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT_val)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

# A column-by-column  
A = torch.empty(B_val, H_val, NT, BT_val, BT_val, dtype=torch.float32, device=k_r.device)
for i in range(BT_val):
    g_i = g_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    A[..., i] = (k_r * (g_r - g_i).exp() * k_i).sum(-1).squeeze(-1)

# Compare with reference A
A_ref = torch.zeros(B_val, H_val, NT, BT_val, BT_val, dtype=torch.float32, device=k_r.device)
for i in range(BT_val):
    g_i = g_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    A_ref[..., i] = torch.einsum('... c d, ... d -> ... c', k_r * (g_r - g_i).exp(), k_i.squeeze(-2))

print(f'A diff (col approach vs ref einsum): {(A - A_ref).abs().max():.10f}')

# Apply mask
mask_diag_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT_val, BT_val, dtype=torch.bool, device=A.device), diagonal=0)
A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A = -A.masked_fill(mask_diag_upper, 0.0)
A_ref = A_ref * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A_ref = -A_ref.masked_fill(mask_diag_upper, 0.0)

print(f'A diff after mask: {(A - A_ref).abs().max():.10f}')

# Cumulative correction (without clone)
for i in range(1, BT_val):
    A_row = A[..., i, :, None]
    A_left = A[..., :, :i]
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
    A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i] + delta

for i in range(1, BT_val):
    A_ref[..., i, :i] = A_ref[..., i, :i].clone() + (A_ref[..., i, :, None].clone() * A_ref[..., :, :i].clone()).sum(-2)

print(f'A diff after correction: {(A - A_ref).abs().max():.10f}')

A = (A + torch.eye(BT_val, dtype=torch.float32, device=A.device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A_ref = (A_ref + torch.eye(BT_val, dtype=torch.float32, device=A_ref.device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
print(f'A diff after final: {(A - A_ref).abs().max():.10f}')

w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)
w_ref = torch.matmul(A_ref, k_exp)
u_ref = torch.matmul(A_ref, v_r)
print(f'w diff: {(w - w_ref).abs().max():.10f}')
print(f'u diff: {(u - u_ref).abs().max():.10f}')

import torch
from einops import rearrange
import reference
import solution

device = torch.device('cuda:0')

# Replicate check.py exactly
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
base_inputs = [t.to(device) if hasattr(t, 'to') else t for t in reference.get_inputs()]

q, k, v, g, beta = base_inputs
q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

scale = float(K) ** -0.5

# Run reference
with torch.no_grad():
    ref_out = reference._naive_chunk_kda(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=scale, chunk_size=64)

# Run solution
with torch.no_grad():
    sol_out = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=scale, chunk_size=64)

diff = (ref_out.float() - sol_out.float()).abs()
print(f'Max diff: {diff.max():.8f}')

# Now let me manually compare A, w, u, etc step by step
qf, kf, vf, gf, betaf = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
qf = qf * scale
BT = 64

q_r = rearrange(qf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(kf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(vf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(gf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(betaf, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

# Reference A
A_ref = torch.zeros(B, H, T//BT, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for i in range(BT):
    g_i = g_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    A_ref[..., i] = torch.einsum('... c d, ... d -> ... c', k_r * (g_r - g_i).exp(), k_i.squeeze(-2))

# My computed A (same as reference)
A_mine = torch.empty(B, H, T//BT, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for i in range(BT):
    g_i = g_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    A_mine[..., i] = torch.einsum('... c d, ... d -> ... c', k_r * (g_r - g_i).exp(), k_i.squeeze(-2))

print(f'A diff: {(A_ref - A_mine).abs().max():.10f}')

# Now do the cumulative correction on both
A_ref_masked = A_ref * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A_ref_masked = -A_ref_masked.masked_fill(torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=0), 0.0)
A_mine_masked = A_mine * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A_mine_masked = -A_mine_masked.masked_fill(torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=0), 0.0)

for i in range(1, BT):
    A_ref_masked[..., i, :i] = A_ref_masked[..., i, :i].clone() + (A_ref_masked[..., i, :, None].clone() * A_ref_masked[..., :, :i].clone()).sum(-2)
for i in range(1, BT):
    A_row = A_mine_masked[..., i, :, None]
    A_left = A_mine_masked[..., :, :i]
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
    A_mine_masked[..., i, :i] = A_mine_masked[..., i, :i] + delta

A_ref_final = (A_ref_masked + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A_mine_final = (A_mine_masked + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)

k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
w_ref = torch.matmul(A_ref_final, k_exp)
w_mine = torch.matmul(A_mine_final, k_exp)
u_ref = torch.matmul(A_ref_final, v_r)
u_mine = torch.matmul(A_mine_final, v_r)

print(f'w diff: {(w_ref - w_mine).abs().max():.10f}')
print(f'u diff: {(u_ref - u_mine).abs().max():.10f}')
