import torch
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

scale = float(K) ** -0.5
qf, kf, vf, gf, betaf = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
qf = qf * scale

q_r = rearrange(qf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(kf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(vf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(gf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(betaf, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

# Compute A, w, u (same as reference)
NT = T // BT
A = torch.empty(B, H, NT, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for i in range(BT):
    g_i = g_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    A[..., i] = torch.einsum('... c d, ... d -> ... c', k_r * (g_r - g_i).exp(), k_i.squeeze(-2))

A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
mask_diag_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=0)
A = -A.masked_fill(mask_diag_upper, 0.0)
for i in range(1, BT):
    A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i].clone() + (A[..., i, :, None].clone() * A[..., :, :i].clone()).sum(-2)

A = (A + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)

k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)
q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

# Inter-chunk: reference version (with clone, einsum, rearrange)
S_ref = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
o_ref = torch.zeros_like(v_r)
mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=1)

for i in range(NT):
    q_i = q_r[:, :, i]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, i]
    u_i = u[:, :, i]
    g_i = g_r[:, :, i]
    w_i = w[:, :, i]
    
    Aqk = torch.zeros(B, H, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
    for j in range(BT):
        k_j = k_i[:, :, j, :]
        g_j = g_i[:, :, j:j+1, :]
        Aqk[..., j] = torch.einsum('... c d, ... d -> ... c', q_i * (g_i - g_j).exp(), k_j)
    Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
    
    v_ref = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S_ref)
    o_ref[:, :, i] = torch.matmul(q_i * g_i.exp(), S_ref) + torch.matmul(Aqk, v_ref)
    
    S_ref = S_ref * rearrange(g_i[:, :, -1].exp(), 'b h k -> b h k 1')
    S_ref = S_ref + rearrange((g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp() * k_i, 'b h c k -> b h k c') @ v_ref

# Inter-chunk: solution version (with .sum(), .transpose())
S_sol = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
o_sol = torch.zeros_like(v_r)

for i in range(NT):
    q_i = q_r[:, :, i]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, i]
    u_i = u[:, :, i]
    g_i = g_r[:, :, i]
    w_i = w[:, :, i]
    q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]
    
    # Solution's Aqk
    Aqk_sol = torch.empty(B, H, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
    for j in range(BT):
        g_j = g_i[:, :, j:j+1, :]
        k_j = k_i[:, :, j:j+1, :]
        Aqk_sol[..., j] = (q_i * (g_i - g_j).exp() * k_j).sum(-1).squeeze(-1)
    Aqk_sol = Aqk_sol.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)
    
    v_sol = u_i - torch.matmul(w_i, S_sol)
    o_sol[:, :, i] = torch.matmul(q_exp_i, S_sol) + torch.matmul(Aqk_sol, v_sol)
    
    g_exp_last = g_i[:, :, -1].exp()
    S_sol = S_sol * g_exp_last.unsqueeze(-1)
    g_diff = (g_i[:, :, -1:] - g_i).exp()
    S_sol = S_sol + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff).transpose(-2, -1), v_sol)

# Compare Aqk
print(f'Aqk diff: {(Aqk - Aqk_sol).abs().max():.10f}')

    A_r[..., i] = torch.einsum('... c d, ... d -> ... c', k_ref * (g_ref - g_i).exp(), k_i.squeeze(-2))

import torch
from einops import rearrange

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

q2 = (q.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

scale = float(K) ** -0.5
qf, kf, vf, gf, betaf = (x.to(torch.float32) for x in (q2, k2, v2, g, beta))
qf = qf * scale

q_r = rearrange(qf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(kf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(vf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(gf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(betaf, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

# Build A (same method for both)
A = torch.empty(B, H, T//BT, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
for i in range(BT):
    g_i = g_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    A[..., i] = torch.einsum('... c d, ... d -> ... c', k_r * (g_r - g_i).exp(), k_i.squeeze(-2))

A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A = -A.masked_fill(torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=0), 0.0)

# Version 1: with clone (reference)
A1 = A.clone()
for i in range(1, BT):
    A1[..., i, :i] = A1[..., i, :i].clone() + (A1[..., i, :, None].clone() * A1[..., :, :i].clone()).sum(-2)

# Version 2: without clone (my solution)
A2 = A.clone()
for i in range(1, BT):
    A_row = A2[..., i, :, None]
    A_left = A2[..., :, :i]
    delta = (A_row * A_left).sum(-2)
    A2[..., i, :i] = A2[..., i, :i] + delta

print(f'A diff (clone vs no-clone): {(A1 - A2).abs().max():.10f}')

# OK so they're identical. Let me now compute the full pipeline with clone
# vs without clone for the inter-chunk part

k_exp = k_r * g_r.exp()
q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

A_final1 = (A1 + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
A_final2 = (A2 + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)

w1 = torch.matmul(A_final1, k_exp)
u1 = torch.matmul(A_final1, v_r)
w2 = torch.matmul(A_final2, k_exp)
u2 = torch.matmul(A_final2, v_r)

print(f'w diff: {(w1 - w2).abs().max():.10f}')

        u = u1.clone()
    else:
        A_final = A_final2.clone()
        w = w2.clone()
        u = u2.clone()
    
    S = torch.zeros(B, H, K, V, dtype=torch.float32, device=device)
    o = torch.zeros_like(v_r)
    mask_strict_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=1)
    
    for i in range(NT):

        k_i = k_r[:, :, i]
        u_i = u[:, :, i]
        g_i = g_r[:, :, i]
        w_i = w[:, :, i]
        q_exp_i = q_exp[:, :, i]

        Aqk = Aqk.masked_fill(mask_strict_upper, 0.0)

        S = S + torch.matmul((k_i * g_diff).transpose(-2, -1), v_ref)

import torch
from einops import rearrange
import reference

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 1024, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

torch.manual_seed(42)
torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(42)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

k2 = (k.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)
v2 = (v.float() * 2.0).to(torch.bfloat16)

scale = float(K) ** -0.5

# Full reference (fp32)
with torch.no_grad():
    ref_out = reference._naive_chunk_kda(q2, k2, v2, g, beta, scale=scale, chunk_size=64)

# Now compute using fp64 for the critical parts

qf = qf * scale

q_r = rearrange(qf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
k_r = rearrange(kf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
v_r = rearrange(vf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
g_r = rearrange(gf, 'b (n c) h d -> b h n c d', c=BT)
beta_r = rearrange(betaf, 'b (n c) h -> b h n c', c=BT)
g_r = g_r.cumsum(-2)

q_exp = q_r * g_r.exp()

A = torch.empty(B, H, T//BT, BT, BT, dtype=torch.float64, device=device)
for i in range(BT):
    g_i = g_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, :, i:i+1, :]
    A[..., i] = torch.einsum('... c d, ... d -> ... c', k_r * (g_r - g_i).exp(), k_i.squeeze(-2))

A = A * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
mask_diag_upper = torch.triu(torch.ones(BT, BT, dtype=torch.bool, device=device), diagonal=0)
A = -A.masked_fill(mask_diag_upper, 0.0)

for i in range(1, BT):
    A[..., i, :i] = A[..., i, :i].clone() + (A[..., i, :, None].clone() * A[..., :, :i].clone()).sum(-2)

A = (A + torch.eye(BT, dtype=torch.float64, device=device)) * beta_r.unsqueeze(-1)
w = torch.matmul(A, k_exp)
u = torch.matmul(A, v_r)

    q_i = q_r[:, :, i]
    k_i = k_r[:, :, i]

import triton
import triton.language as tl


# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# Triton kernel: compute A = k_exp @ k_neg.T + mask + beta
# Each block handles one (B,H,N) matrix of shape (C,C)
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

@triton.jit
def compute_A_kernel(
    k_exp_ptr, k_neg_ptr, beta_ptr, A_ptr,
    stride_ke_b, stride_ke_h, stride_ke_n, stride_ke_c, stride_ke_d,
    stride_kn_b, stride_kn_h, stride_kn_n, stride_kn_c, stride_kn_d,
    stride_be_b, stride_be_h, stride_be_n, stride_be_c,
    stride_A_b, stride_A_h, stride_A_n, stride_A_c, stride_A_d,
    C: tl.constexpr, K: tl.constexpr,
    BLOCK_C: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr,
):
    """Compute A = k_exp @ k_neg.T for one (B,H,N) chunk, apply mask and beta."""
    pid = tl.program_id(0)
    # Single block handles one (B,H,N) — each thread handles one (i,j) tile
    offs_i = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_C)
    offs_j = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_C)
    offs_k = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)

    offs = pid
    n = offs % (32 * 8)  # rough — just placeholder
    # We'll use a simpler approach

command (1720 chars)
cd /workspace/problems/02_kda_cutlass && uv run python -c "
import sys
# Run check.py inline without timeout
import torch
import reference
import solution
import shapes

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
all_shapes = shapes.SHAPES
for shape_idx, shape in enumerate(all_shapes):
    for k, v in shape.items():
        setattr(reference, k, v)
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()
    ref_model = reference.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
    sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()
    sd = ref_model.state_dict()
    sol_model.load_state_dict(sd, strict=True)
    
    for seed in (42, 123, 456):
        torch.manual_seed(seed)
        torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(seed)
        base_inputs = [t.to(device) if hasattr(t, 'to') else t for t in reference.get_inputs()]
        
        # Test nominal and large_qkv
        for scale_input in [1.0, 2.0]:
            q, k, v, g, beta = base_inputs
            if scale_input > 1.0:
                q = (q.float() * scale_input).to(torch.bfloat16)
                k = (k.float() * scale_input).to(torch.bfloat16)
                v = (v.float() * scale_input).to(torch.bfloat16)
            inputs = [q, k, v, g, beta]
            
            with torch.no_grad():
                ref_out = ref_model(*inputs)
                sol_out = sol_model(*inputs)
            
            diff = (ref_out.float() - sol_out.float()).abs()
            max_diff = diff.max().item()
            bad = ((diff > 0.05) & (diff > 0.05 * ref_out.float().abs())).sum().item()
            status = 'PASS' if bad == 0 else f'FAIL ({bad} bad)'
            print(f'Shape {shape_idx} seed {seed} scale={scale_input}: max_diff={max_diff:.6f} {status}')

print('Done')

device = torch.device('cuda:0')

    for k, v in shape.items(): setattr(reference, k, v)
    init_args = reference.get_init_inputs()

    sol_model = solution.Model(*init_args).to(device).eval()

    for seed in (42, 123):
        torch.manual_seed(seed); torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(seed)
        base_inputs = [t.to(device) if hasattr(t,'to') else t for t in reference.get_inputs()]
        for sf in [1.0, 2.0]:

            if sf>1: q=(q.float()*sf).to(torch.bfloat16); k=(k.float()*sf).to(torch.bfloat16); v=(v.float()*sf).to(torch.bfloat16)

import torch
from einops import rearrange
import time

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
B, T, H, K, V = 2, 2048, 8, 128, 128
BT = 64

# Use the same inputs as benchmark
torch.manual_seed(2026)
q = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
k = torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
v = torch.randn(B, T, H, V, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device) * 0.1
g = (torch.randn(B, T, H, K, dtype=torch.float32, device=device) * 0.1 - 0.05)
beta = torch.sigmoid(torch.randn(B, T, H, dtype=torch.bfloat16, device=device))

import solution
with torch.no_grad():
    # Warmup
    for _ in range(5):
        out = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(q, k, v, g, beta, scale=float(K)**-0.5, chunk_size=BT)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    
    # Timed run
    start = time.perf_counter()
    for _ in range(50):
        out = solution._kda_forward_pytorch(q, k, v, g, beta, scale=float(K)**-0.5, chunk_size=BT)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    elapsed = (time.perf_counter() - start) / 50
    print(f'Avg time: {elapsed*1000:.3f} ms')

+from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline
+
+_cuda_src = r"""
+#include <cuda_runtime.h>
+#include <cuda_bf16.h>
+
+using bf16 = __nv_bfloat16;
+
+template<int C, int K, int V>
+__global__ void kda_intra_chunk_kernel(
+    const bf16* __restrict__ k_ptr,
+    const float* __restrict__ g_ptr,
+    const bf16* __restrict__ beta_ptr,
+    const bf16* __restrict__ v_ptr,
+    bf16* __restrict__ w_ptr,
+    bf16* __restrict__ u_ptr,
+    int B, int H, int N,
+    int stride_k_chunk, int stride_k_c, int stride_k_d,
+    int stride_g_chunk, int stride_g_c, int stride_g_d,
+    int stride_b_chunk, int stride_b_c,
+    int stride_v_chunk, int stride_v_c, int stride_v_d,
+    int stride_w_chunk, int stride_w_c, int stride_w_d,
+    int stride_u_chunk, int stride_u_c, int stride_u_d
+) {
+    __shared__ float smem_k[C * K];
+    __shared__ float smem_g[C * K];
+    __shared__ float smem_beta[C];
+    __shared__ float smem_v[C * V];
+    __shared__ float smem_A[C * C];
+    __shared__ float smem_kexp[C * K];
+    __shared__ float smem_kneg[C * K];
+
+    int chunk_id = blockIdx.x;
+    int n = chunk_id % N;
+    int hn = chunk_id / N;
+    int h = hn % H;
+    int batch = hn / H;
+    int tid = threadIdx.x;
+
+    // Load k, g, beta, v into shared memory
+    for (int i = tid; i < C * K; i += blockDim.x) {
+        int c = i / K, d = i % K;
+        int off = batch * stride_k_chunk + h * (N * C * K) + n * (C * K) + c * stride_k_c + d * stride_k_d;
+        smem_k[i] = __bfloat162float(k_ptr[off]);
+    }
+    for (int i = tid; i < C * K; i += blockDim.x) {
+        int c = i / K, d = i % K;
+        int off = batch * stride_g_chunk + h * (N * C * K) + n * (C * K) + c * stride_g_c + d * stride_g_d;
+        smem_g[i] = g_ptr[off];
+    }
+    if (tid < C) {
+        int off = batch * stride_b_chunk + h * (N * C) + n * C + tid * stride_b_c;
+        smem_beta[tid] = __bfloat162float(beta_ptr[off]);
+    }
+    for (int i = tid; i < C * V; i += blockDim.x) {
+        int c = i / V, d = i % V;
+        int off = batch * stride_v_chunk + h * (N * C * V) + n * (C * V) + c * stride_v_c + d * stride_v_d;
+        smem_v[i] = __bfloat162float(v_ptr[off]);
+    }
+    __syncthreads();
+
+    // Cumsum g along last dim
+    for (int c = 1; c < C; c++) {
+        for (int d = tid; d < K; d += blockDim.x) {
+            smem_g[c * K + d] += smem_g[(c-1) * K + d];
+        }
+    }
+    __syncthreads();
+
+    // Compute k_exp = k * exp(g), k_neg = k * exp(-g)
+    for (int i = tid; i < C * K; i += blockDim.x) {
+        float gv = smem_g[i];
+        smem_kexp[i] = smem_k[i] * expf(gv);
+        smem_kneg[i] = smem_k[i] * expf(-gv);
+    }
+    __syncthreads();
+
+    // Compute A = k_neg @ k_exp.T (lower triangle only)
+    for (int i = tid; i < C * C; i += blockDim.x) smem_A[i] = 0.0f;
+    __syncthreads();
+
+    for (int i = 0; i < C; i++) {
+        for (int j = 0; j < C; j++) {
+            if (i <= j) continue; // only lower triangle
+            float sum = 0.0f;
+            for (int d = 0; d < K; d++) {
+                sum += smem_kneg[i * K + d] * smem_kexp[j * K + d];
+            }
+            if (tid == 0) smem_A[i * C + j] = sum * smem_beta[j];
+        }
+    }
+    __syncthreads();
+
+    // Cumulative correction
+    for (int i = 1; i < C; i++) {
+        if (tid < i) {
+            float delta = 0.0f;
+            for (int j = 0; j < C; j++) {
+                delta += smem_A[i * C + j] * smem_A[j * C + tid];
+            }
+            smem_A[i * C + tid] += delta;
+        }
+        __syncthreads();
+    }
+    __syncthreads();
+
+    // A = (A + I) * beta[..., None, :]  (row-wise beta)
+    for (int i = tid; i < C * C; i += blockDim.x) {
+        int r = i / C, col = i % C;
+        float val = (r == col ? 1.0f : 0.0f) + smem_A[i];
+        smem_A[i] = val * smem_beta[r];  // row-wise
+    }
+    __syncthreads();
+
+    // w = A @ k_exp, u = A @ v
+    for (int c = tid; c < C; c += blockDim.x) {
+        for (int d = 0; d < K; d++) {
+            float sum = 0.0f;
+            for (int j = 0; j < C; j++) sum += smem_A[c * C + j] * smem_kexp[j * K + d];
+            int off = batch * stride_w_chunk + h * (N * C * K) + n * (C * K) + c * stride_w_c + d * stride_w_d;
+            w_ptr[off] = __float2bfloat16(sum);
+        }
+        for (int d = 0; d < V; d++) {
+            float sum = 0.0f;
+            for (int j = 0; j < C; j++) sum += smem_A[c * C + j] * smem_v[j * V + d];
+            int off = batch * stride_u_chunk + h * (N * C * V) + n * (C * V) + c * stride_u_c + d * stride_u_d;
+            u_ptr[off] = __float2bfloat16(sum);
+        }
+    }
+}
+""";
+
+_kernel = None
+
+def _get_kernel():
+    global _kernel
+    if _kernel is None:
+        _kernel = load_inline(
+            name="kda_cuda",
+            cpp_sources="",
+            cuda_sources=_cuda_src,
+            functions=["kda_intra_chunk_kernel"],
+            verbose=False,
+        )
+    return _kernel
+
+
+def _kda_forward_cuda(
+    q, k, v, g, beta, scale, chunk_size=64,
+):
+    """CUDA-accelerated KDA forward."""
+    # For now, fall back to PyTorch implementation
+    return _kda_forward_pytorch(q, k, v, g, beta, scale, chunk_size)
